<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Planet Reports Financial Results for Third Quarter of Fiscal 2022 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Delivers Record Third Quarter Revenue of $31.7 Million </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Reaffirms Full Year Revenue Outlook for Fiscal Year 2022 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">End of Period Customer Count Increased 32% Year-Over-Year </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Fully Capitalized Following Receipt of Over $590m in Gross Proceeds from NYSE Debut </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>San Francisco, CA &#150; December</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;13, 2021</B> &#150; Planet Labs PBC (&#147;Planet&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;), a leading
provider of daily data and insights about Earth, today announced financial results for its third fiscal quarter that ended October&nbsp;31, 2021, demonstrating its continued execution and the momentum of its unique data subscription business. Last
week, Planet listed on the New York Stock Exchange under the ticker &#147;PL&#148; following the close of its business combination with dMY Technology Group, Inc. IV, a special purpose acquisition company (dMY IV). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third Quarter FY2022 Financial Highlights: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased 16% year-over-year to $31.7&nbsp;million. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Percent of Recurring Annual Contract Value (ACV) was 94%, compared to 93% in the third quarter of fiscal year
2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">End of Period (EoP) Customer Count increased 32% year-over-year to 742 customers. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Gross Margin percentage expanded to 34%, compared to 27% in the third quarter of fiscal year 2021. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage expanded to 35%, compared to 28% in the third quarter of fiscal year 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net loss was $41.5&nbsp;million and Adjusted EBITDA was ($12.3) million, driven by increased investments in
R&amp;D, sales and marketing and public company costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Definitions of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures used in this press release and reconciliations of such measures to their nearest GAAP equivalents are included below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our strong
performance this past quarter continues to demonstrate Planet&#146;s ability to capture the market opportunity ahead of us,&#148; said Will Marshall, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Founder,</FONT> Chief Executive Officer and Chairperson of
Planet. &#147;With over $590&nbsp;million gross proceeds raised as part of our debut on NYSE last week, we expect that we are fully capitalized to invest in our key growth initiatives, which include expanding our sales force, reinforcing the power
of Planet&#146;s proprietary Earth data, and growing our software organization to expand our analytic solutions. As digital transformation and sustainability continue to drive massive new demands across businesses and governments worldwide,
we&#146;ve never been more confident in Planet&#146;s commercial momentum and opportunity for impact.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ashley Johnson, Planet&#146;s Chief Financial
and Operating Officer added: &#147;We are very excited by both our public listing and our rapidly growing, diversified global customer base. As our financial results demonstrate, Planet&#146;s platform continues to drive tremendous value to
companies in numerous vertical markets. We remain focused on executing against our top line growth plan and capitalizing on the robust demand that we see in the market for Planet&#146;s data. During the third quarter, we achieved sales pipeline
growth of 46% on a year-over-year basis. We see meaningful opportunities to continually create new markets, as well as grow our share in private and public sector customers alike.&#148; </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recent Business Highlights: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Combination Transaction and Public Market Debut: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Planet completed its business combination with dMY IV, raising over $590&nbsp;million in gross proceeds and
listing on the New York Stock Exchange under the ticker &#147;PL&#148;. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

shares. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>New and Expanded Customer Contracts: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Acceleration of Analytics Capabilities: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

report on key conditions on the Earth&#146;s surface, including soil moisture, land surface temperature and vegetation optical depth. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

continue to mature its offerings in other verticals including insurance, civil government, and finance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>New Product
Launches: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

major new products: Pelican and Fusion with SAR. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Pelican is a next-generation fleet of satellites that will provide very high resolution imagery and is planned to
begin launching next year and be operational in 2023. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Fusion with SAR is a cutting-edge data enhancement that will be incorporated into Planet&#146;s existing Fusion
Monitoring product. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Sustainability Initiatives: </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Planet attended and held numerous meetings and events at the United Nations&#146; Climate Change Conference
(COP26) in Glasgow, UK, to discuss strategies to save the planet from the worst effects of the climate emergency, particularly in the areas of forestry and methane emissions - two areas that saw groundbreaking multinational commitments come out of
the conference. Planet detailed how it can provide the data needed to track and report on the ambitious targets set at COP26 and hold national governments and individual actors accountable. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Carbon Mapper, a nonprofit partnering with Planet to deploy a ground-breaking hyperspectral satellite
constellation that would help make reaching these sustainability targets a reality, recently received a $25&nbsp;million investment from Bloomberg Philanthropies, increasing total funding for the partnership to $125&nbsp;million. Planet and NASA JPL
are in the process of building the first two hyperspectral Carbon Mapper satellites that will have the ability to pinpoint, quantify and track point-source methane and CO2 emissions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Education&nbsp;&amp; Research: </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Planet&#146;s robust Education and Research Program led to its satellite data being used in over 1,500 academic
publications since 2016. Notably, in 2021, a study using Planet&#146;s data was published an average of once every 15 hours. The program grew more than 80% since last year, demonstrating the high demand for Planet data in academic settings.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Governance Enhancements: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Planet welcomed two <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT>
members to its Board of Directors as part of its transition to the public markets: Twitter&#146;s Chief Legal Officer, Vijaya Gadde, and Niccolo de Masi, former CEO of dMY Technology Group, Inc. IV. Their extensive expertise across technology,
operations, and public markets are expected to complement strong skill sets already on Planet&#146;s Board and support the company&#146;s continued success. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the fourth quarter of fiscal 2022,
Planet expects to continue to invest in scaling its sales organization and expanding its software engineering capabilities. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Planet currently expects
revenue to be in the range of approximately $35&nbsp;million to $37&nbsp;million and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage to be approximately 37% to 39%. Adjusted EBITDA loss is expected to be between
approximately ($17) million and ($15) million and capex spend is expected to be between approximately $5&nbsp;million and $7&nbsp;million. Additionally, following the business combination with dMY IV, Planet&#146;s pro forma shares outstanding as of
October&nbsp;31, 2021 are approximately 261.8&nbsp;million on a basic and fully diluted basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
measures included in our financial outlook were not reconciled to the comparable GAAP financial measures because the GAAP measures are not accessible on a forward-looking basis. We are unable to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to the most directly comparable GAAP measures without unreasonable efforts because we are currently unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the type and extent of certain
items that would be expected to impact GAAP measures for these periods but would not impact the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Such items may include stock-based compensation charges, depreciation and amortization and
other items. The unavailable information could have a significant impact on our GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The foregoing forward-looking statements reflect
our expectations as of today&#146;s date. Given the number of risk factors, uncertainties and assumptions discussed below, actual results may differ materially. We do not intend to update our financial outlook until our next quarterly results
announcement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Please see &#147;Planet&#146;s Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures&#148; below for a discussion on
how we calculate the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures presented herein. In addition, please find below a reconciliation to the most directly comparable GAAP measure. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Additionally, a supplemental Fiscal 3Q&#146;22 Update presentation has been made available on Planet&#146;s
investor relations page. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Planet </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Planet is a
leading provider of global, daily satellite imagery and geospatial solutions. Planet is driven by a mission to image the world every day, and make change visible, accessible and actionable. Founded in 2010 by three NASA scientists, Planet designs,
builds, and operates the largest Earth observation fleet of imaging satellites, capturing and compiling data from over 3&nbsp;million images per day. Planet provides mission-critical data, advanced insights, and software solutions to over 700
customers, comprising the world&#146;s leading agriculture, forestry, intelligence, education and finance companies and government agencies, enabling users to simply and effectively derive unique value from satellite imagery. Planet is a public
benefit corporation trading on the New York Stock Exchange as PL. To learn more visit www.planet.com and follow us on Twitter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Planet&#146;s Use of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press release includes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross
Margin percentage, which is derived from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Profit (Loss), and Adjusted EBITDA, which are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> performance measures that the Company uses to supplement
its results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage and Adjusted EBITDA are useful in evaluating its operating performance, as they are similar to measures
reported by the Company&#146;s public competitors and are regularly used by analysts, institutional investors, and other interested parties in analyzing operating performance and prospects. Further, the Company believes such <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures are helpful in highlighting trends in the Company&#146;s operating results because they exclude items that are not indicative of the Company&#146;s core operating performance. In addition, the
Company includes these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures because they are used by management to evaluate the Company&#146;s core operating performance and trends and to make strategic decisions regarding the
allocation of capital and new investments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As mentioned above, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Profit (Loss) and Adjusted EBITDA are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures, are additions, and not substitutes for or superior to, measures of financial performance prepared in
accordance with GAAP and should not be considered as an alternative to Gross Profit (Loss), net income, operating income or any other performance measures derived in accordance with GAAP or as an alternative to cash flows from operating activities
as a measure of liquidity. Further, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Profit (Loss) and Adjusted EBITDA are not based on any standardized methodology
prescribed by GAAP and are not necessarily comparable to similarly-titled measures presented by other companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Planet calculates these <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Profit (Loss) and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage</U>: the Company defines and calculates <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Profit (Loss) as Gross Profit (Loss) adjusted for stock-based compensation classified
as cost of revenue, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Margin percentage as the percentage of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Gross Profit (Loss) to revenue. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
Gross Profit (Loss) excludes stock-based compensation, which has recently been, and will continue to be for the foreseeable future, a significant recurring expense for the Company&#146;s business and an important part of its compensation strategy.
</P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted EBITDA</U>: The Company defines and calculates Adjusted EBITDA as net loss before the impact of
interest income and expense, income tax expense and depreciation and amortization, and further adjusted for the following items: stock-based compensation, change in fair value of convertible notes and warrant liabilities, gain or loss on the
extinguishment of debt and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-operating</FONT> income and expenses such as foreign currency exchange gain or loss. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Key Terms </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Percent of Recurring ACV </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with the calculation of several of the key operational and business metrics the Company utilizes, it calculates Annual Contract Value
(&#147;ACV&#148;) for contracts of one year or greater as the total amount of value that a customer has contracted to pay for the most recent 12 month period for the contract. For short-term contracts (contracts less than 12 months), ACV is equal to
total contract value. The Company defines Percent of Recurring ACV as the dollar value of all data subscription contracts and the committed portion of usage-based contracts divided by the total dollar value of all contracts in its ACV Book of
Business at a specific point in time. The Company defines ACV Book of Business as the sum of the ACV of all contracts that are active on the last day of the period pursuant to the effective dates and end dates of such contracts. Planet believes
Percent of Recurring ACV is a useful metric for investors and management to track as it helps to illustrate how much of its revenue comes from customers that have the potential to renew their contracts over multiple years rather than being <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> in nature. In calculating Percent of Recurring ACV, management applies judgment as to which customers have an active contract at a period end for the purpose of determining ACV Book of Business, which is
used as part of the calculation of Percent of Recurring ACV. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>EoP Customer Count </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company defines EoP Customer Count as the total count of all existing customers at the end of the period. It defines existing customers as customers with
an active contract with Planet at the end of the reported period. For the purpose of this metric, the Company defines a customer as a distinct entity that uses its data or services. Planet sells directly to customers, as well as indirectly through
its partner network. If a partner does not provide the end customer&#146;s name, then the partner is reported as the customer. Each customer, regardless of the number of active opportunities with Planet, is counted only once. For example, if a
customer utilizes multiple products of Planet, Planet only counts that customer once for purposes of EoP Customer Count. A customer with multiple divisions, segments, or subsidiaries are also counted as a single unique customer based on the parent
organization or parent account. The Company believes EoP Customer Count is a useful metric for investors and management to track as it is an important indicator of the broader adoption of its platform and is a measure of its success in growing its
market presence and penetration. In calculating EoP Customer Count, management applies judgment as to which customers are deemed to have an active contract in a period, as well as whether a customer is a distinct entity that uses the Company&#146;s
data or services. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

&#147;safe harbor&#148; provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, including, but not limited to, the Company&#146;s ability to capture market opportunity; whether and when the Company will be able to execute on its growth
initiatives; whether the Company will realize any of the potential benefits from its acquisition of VanderSat; whether the Company will be able to successfully build or deploy its satellites, including new satellites that are in development; whether
the experience any new executives or board members may have will result in benefits for Planet; whether the Company will be able to continue to invest in scaling its sales organization and expanding its software engineering capabilities in the
fourth quarter of fiscal 2022; and the Company&#146;s estimated fourth quarter fiscal 2022, revenue, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross profit margin, adjusted EBITDA and capex spend. Forward-looking statements are based on the
Company&#146;s management&#146;s beliefs, as well as assumptions made by, and information currently available to them. Because such statements are based on expectations as to future financial and operating results and are not statements of fact,
actual results may differ materially from those projected. Factors which may cause actual results to differ materially from current expectations include, but are not limited to: the Company&#146;s limited operating history making it difficult to
predict its future operating results; the Company&#146;s expectations that its operating expenses will increase substantially for the foreseeable future; whether the market for the Company&#146;s products and services that is built upon our data
set, which has not existing before, will grow as expected; whether current customers or prospective customers adopt the Company&#146;s platform; whether the Company will be able to compete effectively with the increasing competition in its market
from commercial entities and governments; the Company&#146;s international operations creating business and economic risks that could impact its operations and financial results; the interruption or failure of the Company&#146;s satellite
operations, information technology infrastructure or loss of its data storage, whether by cyber-attacks or other adverse events that limit its ability to perform our daily operations effectively and provide its products and services; whether the
Company experiences any adverse events, such as delayed launches, launch failures, its satellites failing to reach their planned orbital locations, its satellites failing to operate as intended, being destroyed or otherwise becoming inoperable, the
cost of satellite launches significantly increasing and/or satellite launch providers not having sufficient capacity; the Company&#146;s satellites not being able to capture Earth images due to weather, natural disasters or other external factors,
or as a result of its constellation of satellites having restrained capacity; if the Company is unable to develop and release product and service enhancements to respond to rapid technological change, or to develop new designs and technologies for
its satellites, in a timely and cost-effective manner; downturns or volatility in general economic conditions, including as a result of the current <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic or any other outbreak of an infectious
disease; the loss of one or more of the Company&#146;s key personnel, or its failure to attract, hire, retain and train other highly qualified personnel in the future; the Company&#146;s ability to raise adequate capital, including on acceptable
terms, to finance its business strategies; the impact the Company&#146;s indebtedness has on its ability to raise additional capital to fund operations, operate its business and react to changes in the economy or its industry; how rules and
regulations in the Company&#146;s highly regulated industry may impact its business; if the Company fails to maintain effective internal controls over financial reporting at a reasonable assurance level; and the other factors described under the
heading &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in the Registration Statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4</FONT> filed by dMY IV with the Securities and Exchange Commission (SEC) and any subsequent filings with the SEC the Company may make. Copies
of each filing may be obtained from the Company or the SEC. All forward-looking statements reflect the Company&#146;s beliefs and assumptions only as of the date of this press release. The Company undertakes no obligation to update forward-looking
statements to reflect future events or circumstances. The Company&#146;s results for the quarter ended October&nbsp;31, 2021 are not necessarily indicative of its operating results for any future periods. </P>
